# Moon Jar Stories Audio Prompts

Default direction: English-first narration for the demo app, with optional Korean narration available from the language toggle. Use a warm, premium child-safe storyteller voice, gentle bedtime-safe pacing, and no startling effects.

## 해님 달님 / The Sun and the Moon

### Page 001 - sun_moon_001
English narration: In a deep mountain village, two siblings helped Mother wrap warm rice cakes before market day. Steam curled around the room, and every cake smelled like home.
Optional Korean narration: 깊은 산골 마을에 오누이가 어머니와 함께 따끈한 떡을 쌌어요. 하얀 김이 방 안을 감싸고, 떡마다 집 냄새가 포근히 배었지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with safe family warmth; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: warm, slow opening; let the word warm linger

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/sun-and-moon/en/page-001.wav`
Optional Korean narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/sun-and-moon/ko/page-001.wav`
Audio status: `synthetic_draft`

### Page 002 - sun_moon_002
English narration: Mother lifted the basket onto her back. “Watch the house, and watch each other,” she said. The older sister nodded twice, and the younger brother nodded once more.
Optional Korean narration: 어머니가 광주리를 등에 메며 말했어요. “집도 잘 지키고, 서로도 잘 지키렴.” 누나는 두 번 고개를 끄덕였고, 동생은 한 번 더 크게 끄덕였어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with tender responsibility; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: gentle but purposeful

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/sun-and-moon/en/page-002.wav`
Optional Korean narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/sun-and-moon/ko/page-002.wav`
Audio status: `synthetic_draft`

### Page 003 - sun_moon_003
English narration: High in the pines, a tiger watched the road. He did not smile. His eyes followed the basket, and his hungry nose twitched in the cold air.
Optional Korean narration: 높은 소나무 그늘에서 호랑이가 길을 지켜보고 있었어요. 그는 웃지 않았어요. 배고픈 코가 찬 공기 속에서 벌름거리고, 눈은 광주리를 따라 움직였지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with watchful unease; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: lower voice, slow on watched

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/sun-and-moon/en/page-003.wav`

Audio status: `synthetic_draft`

### Page 004 - sun_moon_004
English narration: The tiger stepped onto the path as softly as falling snow. “Good evening, Mother,” he said, in a voice too smooth to trust.
Optional Korean narration: 호랑이는 눈 내리듯 소리 없이 길로 내려왔어요. “어머니, 안녕하시오.” 그는 믿기엔 너무 매끄러운 목소리로 말했지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with quiet threat; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: make tiger dialogue silky but wrong

### Page 005 - sun_moon_005
English narration: Mother remembered her children waiting at home. She tossed one rice cake down the hill. The tiger lunged after it, and Mother ran the other way.
Optional Korean narration: 어머니는 집에서 기다리는 아이들을 떠올렸어요. 떡 하나를 언덕 아래로 던지자, 호랑이가 그쪽으로 몸을 날렸고 어머니는 반대쪽으로 달렸어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with quick courage; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: quickened pace, then breath

### Page 006 - sun_moon_006
English narration: The tiger snapped up the cake, then sniffed Mother’s fallen scarf. He looked toward the cottage lights. “Ah,” he whispered. “Little doors open for familiar voices.”
Optional Korean narration: 호랑이는 떡을 덥석 먹고, 어머니가 떨어뜨린 수건 냄새를 맡았어요. 그러고는 초가집 불빛을 바라보며 속삭였지요. “익숙한 목소리라면 작은 문도 열리겠군.”

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with cold realization; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: whisper the tiger line

### Page 007 - sun_moon_007
English narration: At home, the children counted stars on the paper window. Then came a knock: tap, tap, tap. “Open the door, my children,” called a voice from outside.
Optional Korean narration: 집에서는 오누이가 창호지에 비친 별을 세고 있었어요. 그때 문이 톡, 톡, 톡 울렸어요. “얘들아, 문 열어라.” 밖에서 목소리가 들렸지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with held breath; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: tap the three knocks with pauses

### Page 008 - sun_moon_008

### Page 009 - sun_moon_009

### Page 028 - sun_moon_028
English narration: When the rooster called, the silver rope lowered the children into Mother’s arms. The sun rose, and the moon faded softly, like a secret kept safe.
Optional Korean narration: 닭이 울자 은빛 동아줄은 아이들을 어머니 품으로 내려 주었어요. 해가 떠오르고 달은 안전한 비밀처럼 조용히 옅어졌지요.

## 호랑이와 곶감 / The Tiger and the Persimmon

### Page 001 - tiger_persimmon_001
English narration: At the edge of a sleepy village, a tiger practiced his scariest face in a puddle. The puddle was not impressed.
Optional Korean narration: 졸린 마을 끝에서 호랑이가 물웅덩이에 대고 무서운 얼굴을 연습했어요. 물웅덩이는 조금도 놀라지 않았지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with playful pride; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: comic pride

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/tiger-and-persimmon/en/page-001.wav`

## 흥부와 놀부 / Heungbu and Nolbu

### Page 001 - heungbu_nolbu_001
English narration: Two brothers lived in one village: Heungbu, whose bowl was small but whose door was open, and Nolbu, whose barns were full but whose shutters stayed shut.
Optional Korean narration: 한 마을에 두 형제가 살았어요. 흥부는 그릇은 작아도 문은 열려 있었고, 놀부는 곳간은 가득해도 덧문은 꼭 닫혀 있었지요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with clear moral texture; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: balanced contrast

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/heungbu-and-nolbu/en/page-001.wav`
Optional Korean narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/heungbu-and-nolbu/ko/page-001.wav`
Audio status: `synthetic_draft`

### Page 002 - heungbu_nolbu_002
English narration: When a hungry neighbor came by and whispered, “Any crumb to spare?” Heungbu shared half a rice ball. It was not much. It was also all he had.
Optional Korean narration: 배고픈 이웃이 찾아와 “부스러기라도 조금 있을까요?” 하고 속삭였어요. 흥부는 주먹밥 반쪽을 나누었지요. 많은 건 아니었어요. 하지만 그에게 있는 전부였답니다.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with tender sacrifice; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: soft emphasis on all

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/heungbu-and-nolbu/en/page-002.wav`

### Page 001 - red_bean_grandma_001

## 심청전 / The Tale of Simcheong

### Page 001 - simcheong_001
English narration: In the misty harbor village, first, Simcheong warmed her father's hands around a rice bowl while gulls cried over the harbor. "Lean on me," Simcheong whispered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 안개 낀 바닷가 마을에서 심청은 아버지의 손을 밥그릇 곁에 따뜻하게 모아 드렸어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 다정한 책임감이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with tender responsibility; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/simcheong/en/page-001.wav`
Optional Korean narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/simcheong/ko/page-001.wav`
Audio status: `synthetic_draft`

### Page 005 - simcheong_005
English narration: In the misty harbor village, before dawn, Simcheong warmed her father's hands around a rice bowl while gulls cried over the harbor. "Lean on me," Simcheong whispered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 안개 낀 바닷가 마을에서 심청은 아버지의 손을 밥그릇 곁에 따뜻하게 모아 드렸어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 다정한 책임감이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 토끼와 자라 / The Rabbit and the Turtle

### Page 001 - rabbit_turtle_001
English narration: At the piney shore, first, Rabbit tasted clover while Turtle watched the road between reeds. "Why me?" Rabbit asked. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 소나무 물가에서 토끼는 토끼풀을 먹고 자라는 갈대 사이 길을 보았어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 궁금하지만 조심스러운 마음이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with curious caution; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

## 도깨비 방망이 / The Dokkaebi Club

### Page 001 - dokkaebi_club_001
English narration: On a pine mountain path, first, the wood gatherer saved the straightest sticks for an old neighbor's cold room. "Who drums in the trees?" he wondered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 소나무 산길에서 나무꾼은 추운 이웃 방을 위해 곧은 장작을 남겼어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 따뜻한 성실함이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 단군 이야기 / The Story of Dangun

### Page 001 - dangun_001
English narration: On the sacred mountain, first, Hwanung opened the cloud gate and listened to people below asking for fair weather. "Teach us," Tiger added. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 신성한 산에서 환웅은 구름문을 열고 사람들의 바람을 들었어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 경이로움이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with awe; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

### Page 012 - dangun_012
English narration: Inside the dim cave, next, Tiger scratched a line in the dust, then another, then wished lines were doors. "The path is still here," Bear answered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.

## 은혜 갚은 까치 / The Grateful Magpie

### Page 001 - grateful_magpie_001
English narration: On an old pine mountain road, first, the traveler shared crumbs beneath a pine without knowing who watched. "Kka-chi," called the bird. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 오래된 소나무 산길에서 나그네는 누가 보는지도 모르고 솔밑에 부스러기를 나누었어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 평화로운 귀 기울임이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with peaceful attention; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

### Page 023 - grateful_magpie_023
English narration: At the temple bell, quietly, the old wall cracked where he had been sleeping moments before. "You remembered," he whispered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.

## 콩쥐팥쥐 / Kongjwi and Patjwi

### Page 001 - kongjwi_patjwi_001
English narration: In the hanok courtyard, first, Kongjwi swept the courtyard while Patjwi counted persimmons from the shade. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 콩쥐와 팥쥐가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 콩쥐와 팥쥐가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 외로운 단단함이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with lonely resilience; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

### Page 014 - kongjwi_patjwi_014
English narration: In the village festival road, next, Patjwi's silk ribbon flashed at the gate. "Tell me the truth," someone said. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.

## 금강산 호랑이 / The Tiger of Geumgang Mountain

### Page 001 - geumgang_tiger_001
English narration: Below bright Geumgang cliffs, first, Grandmother taught the child to greet the mountain before gathering pine cones. "To whom?" asked the child. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 밝은 금강산 바위 아래에서 할머니는 솔방울을 줍기 전 산에 인사하라 가르쳤어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 궁금한 존중이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 혹부리 영감 / The Old Man With a Lump

### Page 001 - lump_old_man_001
English narration: On a village festival path, first, the old man tuned his small drum and touched the lump on his cheek without shame. "Sing the funny one!" children called. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 마을 잔치길에서 할아버지는 작은 북을 맞추고 혹을 부끄러움 없이 만졌어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 따뜻한 자존감이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

### Page 011 - lump_old_man_011
English narration: At the fire circle, first, the chief dokkaebi asked whether the old man wanted the lump lighter. "Yes, if kindness leads," he said. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.

## 견우와 직녀 / Gyeonwu and Jiknyeo

### Page 001 - gyeonwu_jiknyeo_001
English narration: Beside the star river, first, Jiknyeo wove cloud cloth until her fingers shone with moon dust. "Who bells the oxen so gently?" Jiknyeo asked. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 별강 곁에서 직녀는 손끝에 달가루가 빛날 만큼 구름천을 짰어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 고요한 그리움이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

### Page 001 - bari_princess_part_1_001
English narration: In the palace garden, first, Bari's cradle stood behind a silk screen while ministers whispered too loudly. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 바리와 공주가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 바리와 공주가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 묵직한 아픔이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Optional Korean narration: 약꽃와 길가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 약꽃와 길가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 묻는 용기이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 바리공주 2 / Princess Bari Part 2

### Page 001 - bari_princess_part_2_001
English narration: In the misty river, first, the river asked for a song before it would show stepping stones. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 바리와 생명수가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 바리와 생명수가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 조심스러운 놀라움이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with awed caution; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

### Page 002 - bari_princess_part_2_002
English narration: In the misty river, next, Bari sang the nurse's lullaby, and stones rose one by one. "Then walk gently," the elder said. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 바리와 생명수가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 강 곁에서 오래된 약속과 마음의 무게가 드러났어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 조심스러운 놀라움이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 우렁각시 / The Snail Bride

### Page 001 - snail_bride_001
English narration: In the rice fields after rain, first, the farmer came home with mud on his knees and no soup in the pot. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 우렁와 각시가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 우렁와 각시가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 조용한 필요이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 장화홍련 / Janghwa and Hongryeon

### Page 001 - janghwa_hongryeon_001
English narration: In the lotus pond house, first, Janghwa braided Hongryeon's hair where the stepmother's voice could not reach. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.

## 선녀와 나무꾼 / The Fairy and the Woodcutter

### Page 001 - fairy_woodcutter_001
English narration: Deep in the mountain, a woodcutter hid a frightened deer from hunters. Pine wind brushed the spring, and the deer bowed low. "I will remember your kindness," it whispered.
Optional Korean narration: 깊은 산 샘가에서 나무꾼은 사냥꾼에게 쫓기던 사슴을 숨겨 주었어요. 솔바람이 지나가자 사슴은 고개를 숙였지요. “은혜를 잊지 않겠습니다.”

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, culturally grounded, and bittersweet rather than cheerful in consequence scenes.

Target English narration asset: `audio/synthetic-draft/narration/fairy-and-woodcutter/en/page-001.wav`

### Page 002 - fairy_woodcutter_002

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, culturally grounded, and bittersweet rather than cheerful in consequence scenes.

### Page 015 - fairy_woodcutter_015
English narration: The robe became wings again. The fairy lifted one child in each arm. "I must go home," she said, and the woodcutter did not smile.

## 청개구리 이야기 / The Green Frog

### Page 001 - green_frog_001
English narration: In the rain-bright stream bank, first, Mother Frog asked him to sit near the reed, so he hopped to the stone. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 청개구리와 어머니가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 청개구리와 어머니가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 장난스러운 답답함이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with playful frustration; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

## 의좋은 형제 / The Kind Brothers

### Page 001 - kind_brothers_001
English narration: In the two rice barns, first, the brothers stacked rice sacks while moonlight filled the yard. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 형와 동생가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 형와 동생가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 고마운 따뜻함이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with grateful warmth; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.

### Page 001 - farting_daughter_in_law_001

### Page 006 - farting_daughter_in_law_006
English narration: In the hanji room, next, the moon jar trembled when she walked past. "I am still learning," the child answered. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 방귀와 바람가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 배나무 곁에서 오래된 약속과 마음의 무게가 드러났어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 익살스러운 긴장이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

## 구렁덩덩 신선비 / The Gentle Serpent Scholar

### Page 001 - serpent_bridegroom_001
English narration: In the bamboo courtyard, first, three sisters heard of a serpent bridegroom and stepped back. "I will answer carefully," came the reply. Lantern light warmed the hanji doors while pine wind brushed the eaves.
Optional Korean narration: 구렁이와 신선비가 있는 옛이야기 길에서 구렁이와 신선비가 조용히 마주 보며 다음 선택을 생각했어요. 등불과 솔바람, 달그림자와 한지 빛이 마음을 부드럽게 감쌌어요. 그 마음에는 조심스러운 선택이 담겼고, 인물들은 스스로 다음 선택을 바라보았어요.

Direction: English-first warm professional picture-book narration with cautious agency; Korean optional narration should sound natural, musical, and culturally grounded. Read-aloud cue: keep the folktale stakes clear without horror.
